walk-forward validation with a single temporal split.\n   208→        Train on data before the validation period, test on the most recent validation period.\n   209→        This provides an honest OOS performance estimate without leakage.\n   210→        \"\"\"\n   211→        print(\"Running walk-forward validation (single split)...\", flush=True)\n   212→\n   213→        df_sorted = val_rows = int(val_days * 24 * 60 / 15)  # number of 15-min candles\n   218→\n   219→        total_rows = len(df_sorted)\n   220→        if total_rows < val_rows + 1000:\n   221→            print(\"Insufficient data for walk-forward split.\", flush=True)\n   222→            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n   223→\n   224→        # Split: validation = most recent val_rows, training = older data\n   225→        valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[-val_rows:].copy()\n   226→        train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:-val_rows].copy()\n   227→\n   228→        # Limit training samples to most recent MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES (controls memory/time)\n   229→        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   230→            train_df = {len(train_df)} samples, Validation: {len(valid_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n   234→\n   235→        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n   236→        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n   237→        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n   238→        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n   239→\n   240→        # Evolve a fresh population on the training set\n   241→        pop = Population(\n   242→            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n   243→            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n   244→            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n   245→            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n   246→            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n   247→        )\n   248→        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n   249→\n   250→        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n   251→            print(f\"  Generation {gen+1}/{ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION}\", flush=True)\n   252→            # Evaluate individuals on training data\n   253→            for ind in pop.individuals:\n   254→                try:\n   255→                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n   256→                    # Use training accuracy as fitness for selection\n   257→                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n   258→                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n   259→                except Exception as e:\n   260→                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   261→                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   262→\n   263→            # Evolve to next generation, but not after the final generation\n   264→            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n   265→                print(\"  Evolving to next generation...\", flush=True)\n   266→                pop.evolve()\n   267→                best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   268→                print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   269→            else:\n   270→                # Final generation: no evolution, just report best\n   271→                best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   272→                print(f\"    Final best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   273→\n   274→        # Prepare close prices for simulation (used later and here)\n   275→        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n   276→\n   277→        # Re-score individuals on validation set using Sharpe (profitability)\n   278→        print(\"Re-scoring population on validation set (Sharpe-based)...\", flush=True)\n   279→        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   280→            # Skip individuals that failed training\n   281→            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n   282→                print(f\"  Skipping individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} (failed training)\", flush=True)\n   283→                continue\n   284→            try:\n   285→                print(f\"  Rescoring individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   286→                # Predict on validation\n   287→                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n   288→                # Ensure pred_valid is a Series with index\n   289→                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n   290→                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n   291→                # Create signals series aligned to close_prices (fill missing with -1)\n   292→                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n   293→                # Run simulation\n   294→                self.trader.run(signals_ind, close_prices)\n   295→                v_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n   296→                # Use Sharpe as fitness (higher is better)\n   297→                ind.fitness = v_metrics.get('sharpe', -1000)\n   298→                print(f\"    -> Sharpe: {ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   299→                # Preserve validation metrics for later analysis if needed\n   300→                ind.validation_metrics = v_metrics\n   301→            except Exception as e:\n   302→                print(f\"  Validation rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   303→                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   304→\n   305→        # Get top diverse models based on validation Sharpe\n   306→        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n   307→\n   308→        # Generate consensus signals on validation set\n   309→        consensus = ConsensusGate(\n   310→            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n   311→            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n   312→        )\n   313→        signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n   314→\n   315→        # Align close prices (indices correspond)\n   316→        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n   317→\n   318→        # Run simulator on signals\n   319→        self.trader.run(signals, close_prices)\n   320→        metrics = metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signals[mask] == y_valid[mask]).mean()\n   326→        else:\n   327→            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n   328→\n   329→        metrics[\"n_folds\"] = 1\n   330→        print(f\"Walk-forward results: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, Sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.4f}\", flush=True)\n   331→\n   332→        return metrics\n   333→\n   334→    def train_best_models(\n   335→        self,\n   336→        df: pd.DataFrame,\n   337→        population: Population,\n   338→        horizon_data: dict = None\n   339→    ):\n   340→        \"\"\"\n   341→        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n   342→        \"\"\"\n   343→        print(\"Training best models   \"\"\"\n        print(\"Preparing features...\", flush=True)\n\n        # Clean data\n        df = clean_data(df)\n\n        # Create target (next 15-minute direction)\n        df = print(f\"      -> training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n            # Evolve to next generation, but not after the final generation\n            if gen < {best.fitness:.4f} (model={best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n\n        return pop\n\n    def run_walk_forward(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Run walk-forward validation with a single temporal split.\n        Train on data before the validation period, test on the most recent validation period.\n        This provides an honest OOS performance estimate without leakage.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Running walk-forward validation (single split)...\", flush=True)\n\n        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n\n        # Determine validation period length (e.g., 7 days)\n        val_days = ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS\n        val_rows = int(val_days * 24 * 60 / 15)  # number of 15-min candles\n\n        total_rows = len(df_sorted)\n        if total_rows < val_rows + 1000:\n            print(\"Insufficient data for walk-forward split.\", flush=True)\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        # Split: validation = most recent val_rows, training = older data\n        valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[-val_rows:].copy()\n        train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:-val_rows].copy()\n\n        # Limit training samples to most recent MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES (controls memory/time)\n        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n            print(f\"Limited training to {len(train_df)} most recent samples\", flush=True)\n\n        print(f\"Train: {len(train_df)} samples, Validation: {len(valid_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n\n        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # Evolve a fresh population on the training set\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n            print(f\"  Generation {gen+1}/{ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION}\", flush=True)\n            # Evaluate individuals on training data\n            for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    # Use training accuracy as fitness for selection\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n            # Evolve to next generation, but not after the final generation\n            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n                print(\"  Evolving to next generation...\", flush=True)\n                pop.evolve()\n                best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n                print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                # Final generation: no evolution, just report best\n                best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n                print(f\"    Final best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n\n        # Prepare close prices for simulation (used later and here)\n        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n\n        # Re-score individuals on validation set using Sharpe (profitability)\n        print(\"Re-scoring population on validation set (Sharpe-based)...\", flush=True)\n        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n            # Skip individuals that failed training\n            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n                print(f\"  Skipping individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} (failed training)\", flush=True)\n                continue\n            try:\n                print(f\"  Rescoring individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n                # Predict on validation\n                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n                # Ensure pred_valid is a Series with index\n                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n                # Create signals series aligned to close_prices (fill missing with -1)\n                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n                # Run simulation\n                self.trader.run(signals_ind, close_prices)\n                v_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n                # Use Sharpe as fitness (higher is better)\n                ind.fitness = v_metrics.get('sharpe', -1000)\n                print(f\"    -> Sharpe: {ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n                # Preserve validation metrics for later analysis if needed\n                ind.validation_metrics = v_metrics\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Validation rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n        # Get top diverse models based on validation Sharpe\n        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n\n        # Generate consensus signals on validation set\n        consensus = ConsensusGate(\n            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n        )\n        signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n\n        # Align close prices (indices correspond)\n        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n\n        # Run simulator on signals\n        self.trader.run(signals, close_prices)\n        metrics = self.trader.metrics.copy()\n\n        # Compute raw accuracy\n        mask = (signals != -1) & y_valid.notna()\n        if mask.any():\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signals[mask] == y_valid[mask]).mean()\n        else:\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n\n        metrics[\"n_folds\"] = 1\n        print(f\"Walk-forward results: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, Sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.4f}\", flush=True)\n\n        return metrics\n\n    def train_best_models(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        population: Population,\n        horizon_data: dict = None\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Training best models on full data...\", flush=True)\n\n        # Use recent data (last N days) for final training\n        recent_days = 60\n        cutoff_time = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=recent_days)\n        recent_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff_time].copy()\n        print(f\"Recent training data: {len(recent_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n\n        X_recent = recent_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_recent = recent_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # Get top models\n        top_models = population.get_diverse_best(n=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE + 2)\n        print(f\"Selected {len(top_models)} top models for retraining\", flush=True)\n\n        # Retrain on full recent data\n        for i, ind in enumerate(top_models):\n            try:\n                print(f\"  Retraining model {i+1}/{len(top_models)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n                ind.model.fit(X_recent, y_recent)\n                print(f\"    Done\", flush=True)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Failed to train {ind.model_type}: {e}\", flush=True)\n\n        # Train horizon ensemble if not provided and if we have multiple horizons\n        if horizon_data is None:\n            horizon_data = {}\n            horizons_to_train = [h for h in FeatureConfig.HORIZONS.keys() if h != \"15m\"]\n            if horizons_to_train:\n                print(f\"Training horizon ensemble for {len(horizons_to_train)} horizons...\", flush=True)\n                for h_name in horizons_to_train:\n                    factor = FeatureConfig.HORIZONS[h_name]\n                    print(f\"  Horizon {h_name} (factor={factor})\", flush=True)\n                    from .data.processor import resample_to_horizon\n                    # Use horizon minutes correctly; but for speed we skip due to minimal HORIZONS\n                    df_horizon = resample_to_horizon(recent_df, recent_days, factor)\n                    print(f\"    Resampled to {len(df_horizon)} rows\", flush=True)\n                    if len(df_horizon) > 100:\n                        df_horizon = create_target(df_horizon, forward_periods=1)\n                        df_horizon = add_technical_indicators(df_horizon)\n                        df_horizon = add_regime_features(df_horizon)\n                        df_horizon = df_horizon.dropna()\n                        print(f\"    Prepared {len(df_horizon)} samples with {len(df_horizon.columns)} features\", flush=True)\n                        horizon_data[h_name] = df_horizon\n                self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n                print(\"Horizon ensemble training complete\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                print(\"No additional horizons to train (HORIZONS only includes 15m)\", flush=True)\n        else:\n self,\n        current_features: pd.DataFrame,\n        use_horizon: bool = True\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate trading signals for the most recent data points.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.top_models is None:\n            raise RuntimeError(\"Models not trained. Call train_best_models first.\")\n\n        signals = self.consensus_gate.decide(self.top_models, current_features)\n        return signals\n\n    def run_online_step(self, new_data: pd.DataFrame = None):\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute one iteration of the online evolution loop.\n\n        This is the main step method called repeatedly by Arbos.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n        print(\"RUNNING ONLINE STEP\", flush=True)\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n\n        # 1. Load/fetch latest data\n        if new_data is None:\n            df = self.load_or_fetch_data()\n        else:\n            df = new_data\n\n        # 2. For online operation, limit to most recent N days to bound runtime\n        if ModelConfig.ONLINE_DATA_DAYS is not None:\n            cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=ModelConfig.ONLINE_DATA_DAYS)\n            df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff].copy()\n            print(f\"Online mode: limited data to last {ModelConfig.ONLINE_DATA_DAYS} days ({len(df)} rows)\", flush=True)\n\n        # 3. Prepare features\n        print(\"[main] Starting feature preparation...\", flush=True)\n        df = self.prepare_features(df)\n        print(f\"[main] Feature preparation complete: {len(df)} rows, {len(self.feature_names)} features\", flush=True)\n\n        # 3. Split into recent data for training and current for prediction\n        # Use last 30 days for training, current for signal generation\n        recent_cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=30)\n        train_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] <= recent_cutoff].copy()\n        current_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] > recent_cutoff].copy()\n\n        # Limit training samples to control memory/time (use most recent samples)\n        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n            print(f\"Limited training to {len(train_df)} most recent samples\", flush=True)\n\n        if len(train_df) < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            print(f\"Insufficient training data: {len(train_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n            return None\n\n        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # 4. Evolve population\n        population = self.evolve_population(X_train, y_train, generations=ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION)\n\n        # 5. Walk-forward validation on historical folds (use recent data to limit folds)\n        if ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS is not None:\n            wf_cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS)\n            df_wf = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= wf_cutoff].copy()\n            print(f\"Using {len(df_wf)} recent samples for walk-forward validation (max {ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS} days)\", flush=True)\n        else:\n            df_wf = df\n        metrics = self.run_walk_forward(df_wf)\n\n        # 6. Train best models on full recent data and prepare horizon ensemble\n        self.train_best_models(df, population)\n\n        # 7. Generate current signals\n        if len(current_df) > 0:\n            current_features = current_df[self.feature_names]\n            signals = self.generate_current_signals(current_features)\n            print(f\"Generated {len(signals)} current signals\", flush=True)\n            latest_signal = signals.iloc[-1] if len(signals) > 0 else None\n            print(f\"Latest signal: {latest_signal} (1=UP, 0=DOWN, -1=NO TRADE)\", flush=True)\n        else:\n            signals = pd.Series()\n            latest_signal = None\n\n        # 8. Save results\n        self._save_results(metrics, population, signals)\n\n        # Compile full result\n        result = {\n            \"timestamp\": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n            \"accuracy\": metrics.get(\"accuracy\", 0.0),\n            \"bets_per_month\": metrics.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0),\n            \"sharpe\": metrics.get(\"sharpe\", 0.0),\n            \"max_drawdown\": metrics.get(\"max_drawdown\", 0.0),\n            \"total_return\": metrics.get(\"total_return\", 0.0),\n            \"latest_signal\": int(latest_signal) if latest_signal is not None else None,\n            \"population_fitness\": {str(i): ind.fitness for i, ind in enumerate(population.get_best(5))}\n        }\n\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n        print(\"STEP COMPLETE\", flush=True)\n        print(f\"Metrics: {json.dumps(result, indent=2)}\", flush=True)\n        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n\n        return result\n\n    def _save_results(self, metrics: dict, population: Population, signals: pd.Series):\n        \"\"\"Save results to disk.\"\"\"\n        timestamp = datetime.utcnow().strftime(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\")\n        run_dir = self.results_dir / timestamp\n        run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n        # Save metrics\n        with open(run_dir / \"metrics.json\", \"w\") as f:\n            json.dump(metrics, f, indent=2)\n\n        # Save signals\n        signals.to_csv(run_dir / \"signals.csv\")\n\n        # Save top models\n        top_models = population.get_best(5)\n        model_dir = run_dir / \"models\"\n        model_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n        for i, ind in enumerate(top_models):\n            try:\n                ind.model.save(str(model_dir / f\"model_{i}_{ind.model_type}.pkl\"))\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"Could not save model {i}: {e}\", flush=True)\n\n        # Save population metadata\n        pop_data = []\n        for ind in population.individuals[:10]:\n            pop_data.append({\n                \"model_type\": ind.model_type,\n                \"params\": ind.params,\n                \"fitness\": float(ind.fitness)\n            })\n        with open(run_dir / \"population.json\", \"w\") as f:\n            json.dump(pop_data, f, indent=2)\n\n        print(f\"Results saved to {run_dir}\", flush=True)\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Entry point for running the trading system.\"\"\"\n    print(\"[main] main() started\", flush=True)\n    system = TradingSystem()\n\n    # Latest signal: {result['latest_signal']}\", flush=True)\n        print(f\"Accuracy: {result['accuracy']:.4f}, Bets/month: {result['bets_per_month']:.2f}\", flush=True)\n    else:\n        print(\"Step did not complete successfully.\", flush=True)\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n","numLines":558,"startLine":1,"totalLines":558}}}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"id":"gen-1773816727-cmJhH41fJx3XO2l8xdnd","type":"message","role":"assistant","container":null,"content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"I see that arbos.py spawns claude subprocesses. It constructs a prompt and runs `claude -p`. That's the loop. But where is the actual trading system invoked? The prompt that arbos.py sends to Claude includes instructions to perform tasks. The Claude's response includes tool calls (like Edit, Bash, etc.). The arbos.py script executes those tool calls.\n\nBut for the trading system to run, the step would need to include a Bash tool call that runs `python -m arbos_trading.main` or similar. That call would block for a long time, and the tool result would return its output after completion.\n\nSo in my current Step 8 invocation, I need to decide: should I run the training now? Usually the loop is: at each step, the agent (me) might modify code/config, then run a test or full evolution, then evaluate results, update state, and loop.\n\nBut how does the system know to do a full evolution run versus just a quick test? The GOAL.md says: \"Evolve a continuous adaptive system...\" and describes the loop.
